## 8\. å½’çº³å’Œé€’å½’ğŸ”—

åœ¨ä¸Šä¸€ç« ä¸­ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬çœ‹åˆ°å½’çº³å®šä¹‰æä¾›äº†åœ¨ Lean ä¸­å¼•å…¥æ–°ç±»å‹çš„å¼ºå¤§æ‰‹æ®µã€‚æ­¤å¤–ï¼Œ æ„é€ å­å’Œé€’å½’å™¨æä¾›äº†åœ¨è¿™äº›ç±»å‹ä¸Šå®šä¹‰å‡½æ•°çš„å”¯ä¸€æ‰‹æ®µã€‚æ ¹æ® [å‘½é¢˜å³ç±»å‹](https://www.leanprover.cn/tp-lean-zh/InductionAndRecursion/PropositionsAndProofs/#--tech-term-_______________) å¯¹åº”å…³ç³»ï¼Œ è¿™æ„å‘³ç€å½’çº³æ³•æ˜¯è¯æ˜çš„åŸºæœ¬æ–¹æ³•ã€‚

`` `deffib : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")â†’[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") :=funx=>Nat.brecOnxfunxf=>(match(motive:=(x:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference"))â†’Nat.belowxâ†’[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference"))xwith|0=>funx=>1|1=>funx=>1|n.[succ](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat.succ in Lean Language Reference").[succ](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat.succ in Lean Language Reference")=>funx=>x.1[+](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Type-Classes/Basic-Classes/#HAdd___mk "Documentation for HAdd.hAdd in Lean Language Reference")x.2.1)f`#printfib ``
```
def fib : Nat â†’ Nat :=
fun x =>
  Nat.brecOn x fun x f =>
    (match (motive := (x : Nat) â†’ Nat.below x â†’ Nat) x with
      | 0 => fun x => 1
      | 1 => fun x => 1
      | n.succ.succ => fun x => x.1 + x.2.1)
      f
```

å½“ Lean é‡åˆ°é€’å½’å®šä¹‰æ—¶ï¼Œå®ƒé¦–å…ˆå°è¯•ç»“æ„é€’å½’ï¼Œå¤±è´¥æ—¶æ‰è¿”å›åˆ°è‰¯åŸºé€’å½’ã€‚Lean ä½¿ç”¨ `decreasing_tactic` æ¥æ˜¾ç¤ºé€’å½’åº”ç”¨ä¼šè¶Šæ¥è¶Šå°ã€‚ ä¸Šé¢ä¾‹å­ä¸­çš„è¾…åŠ©å‘½é¢˜ `x-y<x` åº”è¯¥è¢«è§†ä¸ºè¿™ç§ç­–ç•¥çš„æç¤ºã€‚


æ€»ç»“ï¼š

- å¦‚æœæ²¡æœ‰ `termination_by` ï¼Œåˆ™é€šè¿‡é€‰æ‹©ä¸€ä¸ªå‚æ•°ï¼Œç„¶åä½¿ç”¨ç±»å‹ç±»è§£æä¸ºè¯¥å‚æ•°çš„ç±»å‹åˆæˆä¸€ä¸ªè‰¯åŸºå…³ç³»ï¼Œä»è€Œæ¨å¯¼å‡ºä¸€ä¸ªè‰¯åŸºå…³ç³»ï¼ˆå¦‚æœå¯èƒ½çš„è¯ï¼‰ã€‚

```
def Vect.zipWith.{u_1, u_2, u_3} : {Î± : Type u_1} â†’
```

```
def Vect.zipWith.match_1.{u_1, u_2, u_3} : {Î± : Type u_1} â†’
  {Î² : Type u_2} â†’
    (motive : (x : Nat) â†’ Vect Î± x â†’ Vect Î² x â†’ Sort u_3) â†’
```

## 8.9. ä¸å¯è®¿é—®æ¨¡å¼ğŸ”—

`inductiveImageOf{Î±Î²:Typeu}(f:Î±â†’Î²):Î²â†’Typeuwhere|imf:(a:Î±)â†’[ImageOf](https://www.leanprover.cn/tp-lean-zh/InductionAndRecursion/InductionAndRecursion/#ImageOf "Definition of example")f(fa)` `[open](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Namespaces-and-Sections/#Lean___Parser___Command___open "Documentation for syntax in Lean Language Reference")ImageOf` `definverse{f:Î±â†’Î²}:(b:Î²)â†’[ImageOf](https://www.leanprover.cn/tp-lean-zh/InductionAndRecursion/InductionAndRecursion/#ImageOf "Definition of example")fbâ†’Î±|.(fa),[imf](https://www.leanprover.cn/tp-lean-zh/InductionAndRecursion/InductionAndRecursion/#ImageOf "Definition of example")a=>a` `definverse'{f:Î±â†’Î²}:(b:Î²)â†’[ImageOf](https://www.leanprover.cn/tp-lean-zh/InductionAndRecursion/InductionAndRecursion/#ImageOf "Definition of example")fbâ†’Î±|_,[imf](https://www.leanprover.cn/tp-lean-zh/InductionAndRecursion/InductionAndRecursion/#ImageOf "Definition of example")a=>a`

`inductiveVect(Î±:Typeu):[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")â†’Typeu|nil:VectÎ±0|cons:Î±â†’{n:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")}â†’VectÎ±nâ†’VectÎ±(n+1)` ```defVect.add[[Add](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Type-Classes/Basic-Classes/#Add___mk "Documentation for Add in Lean Language Reference")Î±]:{n:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")}â†’VectÎ±nâ†’VectÎ±nâ†’VectÎ±n|0,nil,nil=>nil|`` unused variable `n`Note: This linter can be disabled with `set_option linter.unusedVariables false` ``n+1,consaas,consbbs=>cons(a+b)(addasbs)```

å‚æ•° `{n:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")}` å‡ºç°åœ¨å†’å·ä¹‹åï¼Œå› ä¸ºå®ƒä¸èƒ½åœ¨æ•´ä¸ªå®šä¹‰ä¸­ä¿æŒå›ºå®šã€‚åœ¨å®ç°æ­¤å®šä¹‰æ—¶ï¼Œ æ–¹ç¨‹ç¼–è¯‘å™¨é¦–å…ˆåŒºåˆ†ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå‚æ•°æ˜¯ `0` è¿˜æ˜¯ `n+1` çš„å½¢å¼ã€‚ æ¥ä¸‹æ¥æ˜¯å¯¹æ¥ä¸‹æ¥çš„ä¸¤ä¸ªå‚æ•°è¿›è¡ŒåµŒå¥—æ¡ˆä¾‹æ‹†åˆ†ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”åœ¨æ¯ç§æƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼Œæ–¹ç¨‹ç¼–è¯‘å™¨éƒ½ä¼šæ’é™¤ä¸ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªæ¨¡å¼ä¸å…¼å®¹çš„æƒ…å†µã€‚
